       <div class="sitenotice" dir="ltr" lang="en">
        <div class="noticebar roundy plainlinks" style="padding:0px;">
         Bulbapedia will be locked from editing on Tuesday November 5th from 03:00 UTC while we perform some server maintenance. We expect the maintenance to span a few days. Updates will be provided via our
         <a class="external text" href="https://x.com/Bulbapedia" rel="nofollow">
          X
         </a>
         account if necessary.
         <br/>
         Please remember to follow the
         <b>
          <a href="/wiki/Bulbapedia:Unreleased_materials_policy" title="Bulbapedia:Unreleased materials policy">
           unreleased materials policy
          </a>
         </b>
         ,
         <b>
          <a href="/wiki/Bulbapedia:Manual_of_style" title="Bulbapedia:Manual of style">
           manual of style
          </a>
         </b>

         <b>
          <a href="/wiki/Bulbapedia:Code_of_conduct" title="Bulbapedia:Code of conduct">

          </a>
         </b>
         at all times.
         <br/>
         Check the
         <a class="external text" href="https://bulbagarden.net/" rel="nofollow">
          Bulbagarden home page
         </a>
         for up-to-date Pokémon news and discuss it on the
         <a class="external text" href="https://forums.bulbagarden.net/index.php" rel="nofollow">
          forums
         </a>
         or in the

         </a>

        <p>
         <b>
          Zacian
         </b>
         (
         <a href="/wiki/List_of_Japanese_Pok%C3%A9mon_names" title="List of Japanese Pokémon names">
          Japanese
         </a>
         :
         <b>
          ザシアン
         </b>
         <i>
          Zacian
         </i>
         ) is a
         <a href="/wiki/Fairy_(type)" title="Fairy (type)">
          Fairy-type
         </a>
         <a href="/wiki/Legendary_Pok%C3%A9mon" title="Legendary Pokémon">
          Legendary Pokémon
         </a>
         introduced in
         <a href="/wiki/Generation_VIII" title="Generation VIII">
          Generation VIII
         </a>
         .
        </p>
        <p>
         While it is not known to
         <a href="/wiki/Evolution" title="Evolution">
          evolve
         </a>
         into or from any other Pokémon, Zacian has a second
         <a href="/wiki/List_of_Pok%C3%A9mon_with_form_differences#Zacian" title="List of Pokémon with form differences">
          form
         </a>
         activated by giving it a
         <a href="/wiki/Rusted_Sword" title="Rusted Sword">
          Rusted Sword
         </a>
         to hold. Its original form,
         <b>
          Hero of Many Battles
         </b>
         , will then become the dual-type
         <a href="/wiki/Fairy_(type)" title="Fairy (type)">
          Fairy
         </a>
         /
         <a href="/wiki/Steel_(type)" title="Steel (type)">
          Steel
         </a>
         <b>
          Crowned Sword
         </b>
         .
        </p>
        <p>
         Zacian is the
         <a href="/wiki/Game_mascot" title="Game mascot">
          game mascot
         </a>
         of
         <a href="/wiki/Pok%C3%A9mon_Sword_and_Shield" title="Pokémon Sword and Shield">
          Pokémon Sword
         </a>
         , appearing on its boxart in its Crowned Sword form. It is a member of the
         <a href="/wiki/Legendary_heroes" title="Legendary heroes">
          legendary heroes
         </a>
         with
         <a href="/wiki/Zamazenta_(Pok%C3%A9mon)" title="Zamazenta (Pokémon)">
          Zamazenta
         </a>
         .
        </p>
        <p>
         It is associated with
         <a href="/wiki/Eternatus_(Pok%C3%A9mon)" title="Eternatus (Pokémon)">
          Eternatus
         </a>
         , playing a role in stopping the
         <a href="/wiki/Darkest_Day" title="Darkest Day">
          Darkest Day
         </a>
         .
        </p>

        <h2>
         <span class="mw-headline" id="Biology">
          Biology
         </span>
        </h2>
        <div class="thumb tleft">
         <div class="thumbinner" style="width:202px;">
          <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Zacian_Zamazenta_dormant.png">
           <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="551" data-file-width="901" decoding="async" height="122" loading="lazy" src="https://archives.bulbagarden.net/media/upload/thumb/5/51/Zacian_Zamazenta_dormant.png/200px-Zacian_Zamazenta_dormant.png" srcset="https://archives.bulbagarden.net/media/upload/thumb/5/51/Zacian_Zamazenta_dormant.png/300px-Zacian_Zamazenta_dormant.png 1.5x, https://archives.bulbagarden.net/media/upload/thumb/5/51/Zacian_Zamazenta_dormant.png/400px-Zacian_Zamazenta_dormant.png 2x" width="200"/>
          </a>
          <div class="thumbcaption">
           <div class="magnify">
            <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Zacian_Zamazenta_dormant.png" title="Enlarge">
            </a>
           </div>
           Zacian's dormant state (right)
          </div>
         </div>
        </div>
        <p>
         In its Hero of Many Battles form, Zacian is a large cyan lupine
         <a href="/wiki/Pok%C3%A9mon_(species)" title="Pokémon (species)">
          Pokémon
         </a>
         with yellow eyes, a tan underside, a lean frame, a pink tail, and pink braids going down the side of its body. Two pink fringes of fur are present on its back. There are battle scars on its shoulders, hips, back, and forehead, which reveal a tan coloration under the blue fur. Half of its left ear is also missing.
        </p>
        <div class="thumb tright">
         <div class="thumbinner" style="width:202px;">
          <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Zacian_Behemoth_Blade_sword.png">
           <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="720" data-file-width="1280" decoding="async" height="113" loading="lazy" src="https://archives.bulbagarden.net/media/upload/thumb/6/6e/Zacian_Behemoth_Blade_sword.png/200px-Zacian_Behemoth_Blade_sword.png" srcset="https://archives.bulbagarden.net/media/upload/thumb/6/6e/Zacian_Behemoth_Blade_sword.png/300px-Zacian_Behemoth_Blade_sword.png 1.5x, https://archives.bulbagarden.net/media/upload/thumb/6/6e/Zacian_Behemoth_Blade_sword.png/400px-Zacian_Behemoth_Blade_sword.png 2x" width="200"/>
          </a>
          <div class="thumbcaption">
           <div class="magnify">
            <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Zacian_Behemoth_Blade_sword.png" title="Enlarge">
            </a>
           </div>
           Zacian's
           <a href="/wiki/Rusted_Sword" title="Rusted Sword">
            sword
           </a>
           transforms so it can use
           <a href="/wiki/Behemoth_Blade_(move)" title="Behemoth Blade (move)">
            Behemoth Blade
           </a>
          </div>
         </div>
        </div>
        <p>
         It is believed to be either the elder sister or rival of
         <a href="/wiki/Zamazenta_(Pok%C3%A9mon)" title="Zamazenta (Pokémon)">
          Zamazenta
         </a>
         . In the past, Zacian was feared and respected by the people of
         <a href="/wiki/Galar" title="Galar">
          Galar
         </a>
         . 3000 years ago, it worked together with Zamazenta and
         <a href="/wiki/Ancient_Galarian_kings" title="Ancient Galarian kings">
          two young humans
         </a>
         to save the region from
         <a href="/wiki/Eternatus_(Pok%C3%A9mon)" title="Eternatus (Pokémon)">
          Eternatus
         </a>
         and the
         <a href="/wiki/Darkest_Day" title="Darkest Day">
          Darkest Day
         </a>
         it created, defeating the Gigantic Pokémon and forcing it back into slumber, which also caused pieces of its body imbued with its power to rain down throughout Galar in the form of
         <a href="/wiki/Wishing_Piece" title="Wishing Piece">
          Wishing Pieces
         </a>
         and
         <a href="/wiki/Wishing_Star" title="Wishing Star">
          Wishing Stars
         </a>
         . It can also turn itself into a statue and slumber for eons alongside Zamazenta in the
         <a href="/wiki/Slumbering_Weald" title="Slumbering Weald">
          Slumbering Weald
         </a>
         . Zacian can also cast illusions, including a projection of itself, even while it slumbers. Additionally, it is capable of flying. Even though it is not capable of
         <a href="/wiki/Dynamax" title="Dynamax">
          Dynamaxing
         </a>
         , Zacian may still go berserk when bombarded by
         <a href="/wiki/Galar_particle" title="Galar particle">
          Galar particles
         </a>
         . As years passed, both Zacian and Zamazenta were forgotten by history, however,
         <a href="/wiki/Sonia" title="Sonia">
          Professor Sonia
         </a>
         proved their existence by writing her first book: "
         <a href="/wiki/Sonia%27s_Book" title="Sonia's Book">
          Galar: A History
         </a>
         ", which details the discovery she and the
         <a href="/wiki/Player_character" title="Player character">
          player
         </a>
         had in
         <a href="/wiki/Stow-on-Side" title="Stow-on-Side">
          Stow-on-Side
         </a>
         .
        </p>
        <p>
         Zacian is the
         <a href="/wiki/Signature_Ability" title="Signature Ability">
          only known Pokémon
         </a>
         that can have
         <a href="/wiki/Intrepid_Sword_(Ability)" title="Intrepid Sword (Ability)">
          Intrepid Sword
         </a>
         as its
         <a href="/wiki/Ability" title="Ability">
          Ability
         </a>
         .
         <br clear="left"/>
        </p>
        <h3>
         <span class="mw-headline" id="Forms">
          Forms
         </span>
        </h3>
        <div class="thumb tright">
         <div class="thumbinner" style="width:302px;">
          <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:7elevenPokemon11Japan.jpg">
           <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="590" data-file-width="970" decoding="async" height="182" loading="lazy" src="https://archives.bulbagarden.net/media/upload/thumb/f/fe/7elevenPokemon11Japan.jpg/300px-7elevenPokemon11Japan.jpg" srcset="https://archives.bulbagarden.net/media/upload/thumb/f/fe/7elevenPokemon11Japan.jpg/450px-7elevenPokemon11Japan.jpg 1.5x, https://archives.bulbagarden.net/media/upload/thumb/f/fe/7elevenPokemon11Japan.jpg/600px-7elevenPokemon11Japan.jpg 2x" width="300"/>
          </a>
          <div class="thumbcaption">
           <div class="magnify">
            <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:7elevenPokemon11Japan.jpg" title="Enlarge">
            </a>
           </div>
           Crowned Sword Zacian with a sheathed sword from 7-Eleven Japan artwork
          </div>
         </div>
        </div>
        <p>
         Zacian has two forms: Hero of Many Battles and Crowned Sword.
        </p>
        <p>
         Zacian can change to its Crowned Sword form in battle by wielding its
         <a href="/wiki/Rusted_Sword" title="Rusted Sword">
          Rusted Sword
         </a>
         , absorbing metal particles in the air, and using them to form a golden armor over its body and transforming its ancient weapon into a large, golden sword.
        </p>
        <p>
         In its Crowned Sword form, the fringes of fur on its back become wing-like armor and its braids grow to resemble ribbons. Additionally, its head is covered by a golden helmet, and it carries a golden sword decorated to resemble Zacian's colors; when using the move
         <a href="/wiki/Behemoth_Blade_(move)" title="Behemoth Blade (move)">
          Behemoth Blade
         </a>
         , the armor on Zacian's back combines with the sword to increase its size and power.
        </p>
        <p>
         Zacian can sheathe its sword when not in use by wrapping it with its mane. Crowned Sword is Zacian's true form, and it is at its full power in this form. It is capable of cutting down anything in one strike, and its skills inspired awe in both its friends and foes. When together with
         <a href="/wiki/Zamazenta_(Pok%C3%A9mon)" title="Zamazenta (Pokémon)">
          Zamazenta
         </a>
         in their Crowned forms, it can negate the mysterious power of
         <a href="/wiki/Eternamax" title="Eternamax">
          Eternamax
         </a>
         <a href="/wiki/Eternatus_(Pok%C3%A9mon)" title="Eternatus (Pokémon)">
          Eternatus
         </a>
         , which prevents opposing Pokémon from attacking it.
        </p>
        <p>
         Zacian attacks with graceful, swift, and captivating movements, which have been compared to a dance. It unleashes quick slashes that cannot be seen by the naked eye; those struck by its sword will be cut down before they can feel the pain. The sword it holds in its mouth can cut through anything, even the thick scales of
         <a href="/wiki/Dragon_(type)" title="Dragon (type)">
          Dragon-type
         </a>
         Pokémon, as if they were paper. According to legends, in this form, it was known as the "
         <b>
          Fairy King's Sword
         </b>
         ", due to its Typing and weapon.
        </p>
        <p>
         Crowned Sword Zacian is the
         <a href="/wiki/Signature_move" title="Signature move">
          only known Pokémon
         </a>
         capable of using the move
         <a href="/wiki/Behemoth_Blade_(move)" title="Behemoth Blade (move)">
          Behemoth Blade
         </a>
         . When using Behemoth Blade, it is said to be able to cut the ocean in two.
         <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-1">
          <a href="#cite_note-1">
           [1]
          </a>
         </sup>
        </p>

               </td>
              </tr>
              <tr>
               <td style="line-height:90%; font-size: 90%;">
                <ul>
                 <li>
                  If this Pokémon is given a
                  <a href="/wiki/Ring_Target" title="Ring Target">
                   <span style="color:#000;">
                    Ring Target
                   </span>
                  </a>
                  , the effectiveness of
                  <span style="background: #9141CB">
                   <a href="/wiki/Poison_(type)" title="Poison (type)">
                    <span style="color:#FFFFFF;">
                     Poison-type
                    </span>
                   </a>
                  </span>
                  moves is 2×.
                 </li>
                 <li>
                  If this Pokémon is given a
                  <a href="/wiki/Ring_Target" title="Ring Target">
                   <span style="color:#000;">
                    Ring Target
                   </span>
                  </a>
                  , the effectiveness of
                  <span style="background: #5060E1">
                   <a href="/wiki/Dragon_(type)" title="Dragon (type)">
                    <span style="color:#FFFFFF;">
                     Dragon-type
                    </span>
                   </a>
                  </span>
                  moves is ½×.
                 </li>
                </ul>
               </td>
              </tr>
             </tbody>
            </table>
           </td>
          </tr>
         </tbody>

               <td style="background:#FFFFFF; text-align:center; border:1px solid #D8D8D8;">
                5
               </td>
              </tr>
             </tbody>
            </table>
           </td>
          </tr>
          <tr>
           <td class="roundybottom" colspan="7" style="background:#F5A2F5; font-size: 90%; line-height:10px;">
            <ul>
             <li>
              <b>
               Bold
              </b>
              indicates a move that gets
              <a href="/wiki/Same-type_attack_bonus" title="Same-type attack bonus">
               <span style="color:#000;">
                STAB
               </span>
              </a>
              when used by Zacian
             </li>
             <li>
              <i>
               Italic
              </i>
              indicates a move that gets STAB only when used by an Evolution  of Zacian
             </li>
            </ul>
           </td>
          </tr>
         </tbody>
        </table>

        <h4>
         <span class="mw-headline" id="Form_change">
          Form change
         </span>
        </h4>
        <p>
         If Zacian knows
         <a href="/wiki/Iron_Head_(move)" title="Iron Head (move)">
          Iron Head
         </a>
         when it enters battle in its Crowned Sword form, Iron Head will become its
         <a href="/wiki/Signature_move" title="Signature move">
          signature move
         </a>
         ,
         <a href="/wiki/Behemoth_Blade_(move)" title="Behemoth Blade (move)">
          Behemoth Blade
         </a>
         , until the battle ends, where it becomes Iron Head again.
         <span id="Form_change">
         </span>
        </p>

        <h3>
         <span class="mw-headline" id="Form_data">
          Form data
         </span>
        </h3>
        <p>
         Zacian has two forms, Hero of Many Battles and Crowned Sword, which change its appearance,
         <a href="/wiki/Stat" title="Stat">
          stats
         </a>
         ,
         <a href="/wiki/Type" title="Type">
          type
         </a>
         , and
         <a href="/wiki/Cry" title="Cry">
          cry
         </a>
         . Zacian will always be in its Hero of Many Battles form outside of
         <a href="/wiki/Pok%C3%A9mon_battle" title="Pokémon battle">
          battle
         </a>
         . In battle, Zacian will be in its Crowned Sword form if it holds a
         <a href="/wiki/Rusted_Sword" title="Rusted Sword">
          Rusted Sword
         </a>
         . In this form, Zacian gains
         <a href="/wiki/Steel_(type)" title="Steel (type)">
          Steel
         </a>
         as a secondary type and has increased
         <a href="/wiki/Stat#Attack" title="Stat">
          Attack
         </a>
         and
         <a href="/wiki/Stat#Speed" title="Stat">
          Speed
         </a>
         . Additionally, if Zacian knows
         <a href="/wiki/Iron_Head_(move)" title="Iron Head (move)">
          Iron Head
         </a>
         , the move will be replaced with
         <a href="/wiki/Behemoth_Blade_(move)" title="Behemoth Blade (move)">
          Behemoth Blade
         </a>
         .
        </p>
        <div class="scrollbox">
         <table class="roundy" style="margin:auto; text-align:center; background: #EF70EF; border: 3px solid #9B499B;">

        <h4>
         <span class="mw-headline" id="Major_appearances">
          Major appearances
         </span>
        </h4>
        <h5>
         <span id="Zacian_.28anime.29">
         </span>
         <span class="mw-headline" id="Zacian_(anime)">
          <a href="/wiki/Legendary_heroes_(anime)" title="Legendary heroes (anime)">
           Zacian (anime)
          </a>
         </span>
        </h5>
        <p>
         <a href="/wiki/Legendary_heroes_(anime)#Zacian" title="Legendary heroes (anime)">
          Zacian
         </a>
         debuted in its Hero of Many Battles form in
         <i>
          <a href="/wiki/JN042" title="JN042">
           Sword and Shield, Slumbering Weald!
          </a>
         </i>
         .
         <a href="/wiki/Ash_Ketchum" title="Ash Ketchum">
          Ash
         </a>
         encountered it in the
         <a href="/wiki/Slumbering_Weald" title="Slumbering Weald">
          Slumbering Weald
         </a>
         before it disappeared. In
         <i>
          <a href="/wiki/JN044" title="JN044">
           Sword and Shield: "From Here to Eternatus!"
          </a>
         </i>
         , it led
         <a href="/wiki/Goh" title="Goh">
          Goh
         </a>
         and
         <a href="/wiki/Sonia" title="Sonia">
          Sonia
         </a>
         to the altar, where they found the
         <a href="/wiki/Rusted_Sword" title="Rusted Sword">
          Rusted Sword
         </a>
         and
         <a href="/wiki/Rusted_Shield" title="Rusted Shield">
          Shield
         </a>
         . In
         <i>
          <a href="/wiki/JN045" title="JN045">
           Sword and Shield... The Legends Awaken!
          </a>
         </i>
         , Zacian entered its Crowned Sword form and battled
         <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Goh%27s_Eternatus" title="Goh's Eternatus">
          Eternatus
         </a>
         with
         <a href="/wiki/Zamazenta_(Pok%C3%A9mon)" title="Zamazenta (Pokémon)">
          Zamazenta
         </a>
         , defeating it. In the intro segment of
         <i>
          <a href="/wiki/JN046" title="JN046">
           Getting More Than You Battled For!
          </a>
         </i>
         , it was at the altar of the Slumbering Weald.
        </p>

        <h3>
         <span id="GOTCHA.21">
         </span>
         <span class="mw-headline" id="GOTCHA!">
          GOTCHA!
         </span>
        </h3>
        <p>
         A Zacian briefly appeared in its Hero of Many Battles form in
         <a href="/wiki/GOTCHA!" title="GOTCHA!">
          GOTCHA!
         </a>
         .
        </p>
        <h3>
         <span id="Pok.C3.A9mon_Evolutions">
         </span>
         <span class="mw-headline" id="Pokémon_Evolutions">
          Pokémon Evolutions
         </span>
        </h3>
        <div class="thumb tleft">
         <div class="thumbinner" style="width:252px;">
          <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Zacian_Zamazenta_Hero_of_Many_Battles_Evolutions.png">
           <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="1080" data-file-width="1920" decoding="async" height="141" loading="lazy" src="https://archives.bulbagarden.net/media/upload/thumb/2/2d/Zacian_Zamazenta_Hero_of_Many_Battles_Evolutions.png/250px-Zacian_Zamazenta_Hero_of_Many_Battles_Evolutions.png" srcset="https://archives.bulbagarden.net/media/upload/thumb/2/2d/Zacian_Zamazenta_Hero_of_Many_Battles_Evolutions.png/375px-Zacian_Zamazenta_Hero_of_Many_Battles_Evolutions.png 1.5x, https://archives.bulbagarden.net/media/upload/thumb/2/2d/Zacian_Zamazenta_Hero_of_Many_Battles_Evolutions.png/500px-Zacian_Zamazenta_Hero_of_Many_Battles_Evolutions.png 2x" width="250"/>
          </a>
          <div class="thumbcaption">
           <div class="magnify">
            <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Zacian_Zamazenta_Hero_of_Many_Battles_Evolutions.png" title="Enlarge">
            </a>
           </div>
           Zacian in
           <a href="/wiki/Pok%C3%A9mon_Evolutions" title="Pokémon Evolutions">
            Pokémon Evolutions
           </a>
          </div>
         </div>
        </div>
        <div class="thumb tright">
         <div class="thumbinner" style="width:252px;">
          <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Zacian_Crowned_Sword_Evolutions.png">
           <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="1080" data-file-width="1920" decoding="async" height="141" loading="lazy" src="https://archives.bulbagarden.net/media/upload/thumb/4/4a/Zacian_Crowned_Sword_Evolutions.png/250px-Zacian_Crowned_Sword_Evolutions.png" srcset="https://archives.bulbagarden.net/media/upload/thumb/4/4a/Zacian_Crowned_Sword_Evolutions.png/375px-Zacian_Crowned_Sword_Evolutions.png 1.5x, https://archives.bulbagarden.net/media/upload/thumb/4/4a/Zacian_Crowned_Sword_Evolutions.png/500px-Zacian_Crowned_Sword_Evolutions.png 2x" width="250"/>
          </a>
          <div class="thumbcaption">
           <div class="magnify">
            <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Zacian_Crowned_Sword_Evolutions.png" title="Enlarge">
            </a>
           </div>
           Crowned Sword Zacian in Pokémon Evolutions
          </div>
         </div>
        </div>
        <p>
         A Zacian appeared in a flashback in
         <i>
          <a href="/wiki/PE01" title="PE01">
           The Champion
          </a>
         </i>
         , where it entered its Crowned Sword form and battled
         <a href="/wiki/Eternatus_(Pok%C3%A9mon)" title="Eternatus (Pokémon)">
          Eternatus
         </a>
         alongside
         <a href="/wiki/Victor_(game)" title="Victor (game)">
          Victor
         </a>
         ,
         <a href="/wiki/Hop" title="Hop">
          Hop
         </a>
         , and
         <a href="/wiki/Zamazenta_(Pok%C3%A9mon)" title="Zamazenta (Pokémon)">
          Zamazenta
         </a>
         , putting an end to the
         <a href="/wiki/Darkest_Day" title="Darkest Day">
          Darkest Day
         </a>
         .
         <br clear="all"/>
        </p>

        <h3>
         <span id="Pok.C3.A9mon_Adventures">
         </span>
         <span class="mw-headline" id="Pokémon_Adventures">
          Pokémon Adventures
         </span>
        </h3>
        <p>
         Zacian debuted in
         <i>
          <a href="/wiki/PASS05" title="PASS05">
           Ooh Shiny!! Legendary Equipment
          </a>
         </i>
         .
         <a href="/wiki/Henry_Sword" title="Henry Sword">
          Henry
         </a>
         and
         <a href="/wiki/Casey_Shield" title="Casey Shield">
          Casey
         </a>
         encountered it and
         <a href="/wiki/Zamazenta_(Pok%C3%A9mon)" title="Zamazenta (Pokémon)">
          Zamazenta
         </a>
         in the
         <a href="/wiki/Slumbering_Weald" title="Slumbering Weald">
          Slumbering Weald
         </a>
         , though their attempt to fight off the two Pokémon revealed they were merely illusions. It reappeared in
         <i>
          <a href="/wiki/PASS29" title="PASS29">
           GRRR!! The Irrepairable Gears
          </a>
         </i>
         to face
         <a href="/wiki/Eternatus_(Pok%C3%A9mon)" title="Eternatus (Pokémon)">
          Eternatus
         </a>
         , only for it to disappear alongside Zamazenta and Eternatus. It reappeared again to resume its fight with Eternatus in
         <a href="/wiki/PASS41" title="PASS41">
          PASS41
         </a>
         .
        </p>
        <h3>
         <span id="Pok.C3.A9mon_Journeys">
         </span>
         <span class="mw-headline" id="Pokémon_Journeys">
          Pokémon Journeys
         </span>
        </h3>
        <dl>
         <dd>
          <i>
           Main article:
           <a href="/wiki/Legendary_heroes_(anime)" title="Legendary heroes (anime)">
            Zacian (anime)
           </a>
          </i>
         </dd>
        </dl>
        <p>
         <a href="/wiki/Legendary_heroes_(anime)#Zacian" title="Legendary heroes (anime)">
          Zacian
         </a>
         debuted in
         <i>
          <a href="/wiki/JNM13" title="JNM13">
           Sword and Shield... The Legends Awaken! (Part 1)
          </a>
         </i>
         , playing the same role as it did in the animated series.
         <br clear="all"/>
        </p>

        <h2>
         <span class="mw-headline" id="Other_appearances">
          Other appearances
         </span>
        </h2>
        <div class="thumb tright">
         <div class="thumbinner" style="width:152px;">
          <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:UNITE_Zacian.png">
           <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="690" data-file-width="878" decoding="async" height="118" loading="lazy" src="https://archives.bulbagarden.net/media/upload/thumb/a/a3/UNITE_Zacian.png/150px-UNITE_Zacian.png" srcset="https://archives.bulbagarden.net/media/upload/thumb/a/a3/UNITE_Zacian.png/225px-UNITE_Zacian.png 1.5x, https://archives.bulbagarden.net/media/upload/thumb/a/a3/UNITE_Zacian.png/300px-UNITE_Zacian.png 2x" width="150"/>

        <h3>
         <span class="mw-headline" id="Super_Smash_Bros._Ultimate">
          <a href="/wiki/Super_Smash_Bros._Ultimate" title="Super Smash Bros. Ultimate">
           Super Smash Bros. Ultimate
          </a>
         </span>
        </h3>
        <p>
         Zacian appears as part of the Zacian &amp; Zamazenta
         <a class="extiw" href="https://www.ssbwiki.com/Spirit" title="sbw:Spirit">
          Spirit
         </a>
         .
        </p>
        <h3>
         <span id="Pok.C3.A9mon_UNITE">
         </span>
         <span class="mw-headline" id="Pokémon_UNITE">
          <a href="/wiki/Pok%C3%A9mon_UNITE" title="Pokémon UNITE">
           Pokémon UNITE
          </a>
         </span>
        </h3>
        <dl>
         <dd>
          <i>
           Main article:
           <a href="/wiki/Zacian_(UNITE)" title="Zacian (UNITE)">
            Zacian (UNITE)
           </a>
          </i>
         </dd>
        </dl>
        <p>
         Zacian is playable through obtaining a Unite License. It is a melee all-rounder that can only be played in its Crowned Sword form due to always holding its Rusted Sword item.
         <br clear="all"/>
        </p>
        <h2>
         <span class="mw-headline" id="Trivia">
          Trivia
         </span>
        </h2>
        <ul>
         <li>
          Zacian, Zamazenta, and
          <a href="/wiki/Cresselia_(Pok%C3%A9mon)" title="Cresselia (Pokémon)">
           Cresselia
          </a>
          are the only
          <a href="/wiki/Legendary_Pok%C3%A9mon" title="Legendary Pokémon">
           Legendary Pokémon
          </a>
          to have their
          <a href="/wiki/Base_stats" title="Base stats">
           base stats
          </a>
          changed in a
          <a href="/wiki/Generation_IX" title="Generation IX">
           later generation
          </a>
          .
         </li>
         <li>
          Zacian shares the same
          <a href="/wiki/Pok%C3%A9mon_category" title="Pokémon category">
           category
          </a>
          name with its partner
          <a href="/wiki/Zamazenta_(Pok%C3%A9mon)" title="Zamazenta (Pokémon)">
           Zamazenta
          </a>
          . They are both known as the Warrior Pokémon.
         </li>
         <li>
          Zacian, Zamazenta, and
          <a href="/wiki/Eternatus_(Pok%C3%A9mon)" title="Eternatus (Pokémon)">
           Eternatus
          </a>
          are the only Pokémon available in
          <a href="/wiki/Pok%C3%A9mon_Sword_and_Shield" title="Pokémon Sword and Shield">
           Pokémon Sword and Shield
          </a>
          that cannot
          <a href="/wiki/Dynamax" title="Dynamax">
           Dynamax
          </a>
          .
          <ul>
           <li>
            Pokémon
            <a href="/wiki/Transform_(move)" title="Transform (move)">
             transformed
            </a>
            into Zacian, Zamazenta, or Eternatus will also be unable to Dynamax, such as
            <a href="/wiki/Ditto_(Pok%C3%A9mon)" title="Ditto (Pokémon)">
             Ditto
            </a>
            or
            <a href="/wiki/Mew_(Pok%C3%A9mon)" title="Mew (Pokémon)">
             Mew
            </a>
            .
           </li>
          </ul>
         </li>
         <li>
          In
          <a href="/wiki/Generation_VIII" title="Generation VIII">
           Generation VIII
          </a>
          , Crowned Sword Zacian has the highest
          <a href="/wiki/Stat#Attack" title="Stat">
           Attack
          </a>
          stat of all Fairy-type Pokémon.
         </li>
         <li>
          Crowned Sword Zacian has the highest base
          <a href="/wiki/Stat#Speed" title="Stat">
           Speed
          </a>
          stat of all
          <a href="/wiki/Fairy_(type)" title="Fairy (type)">
           Fairy-type
          </a>
          and
          <a href="/wiki/Steel_(type)" title="Steel (type)">
           Steel-type
          </a>
          Pokémon.
          <ul>
           <li>
            Moreover, it is tied with Mega
            <a href="/wiki/Diancie_(Pok%C3%A9mon)" title="Diancie (Pokémon)">
             Diancie
            </a>
            for the highest base stat total of all Fairy-type Pokémon.
           </li>
          </ul>
         </li>
         <li>
          Crowned Sword Zacian is the
          <a href="/wiki/List_of_Pok%C3%A9mon_by_weight" title="List of Pokémon by weight">
           heaviest
          </a>
          Fairy-type Pokémon.
         </li>
         <li>
          Despite being a gender unknown species, Zacian is referred to as Zamazenta's older sister in its English, Japanese, and
          <a href="/wiki/Pok%C3%A9mon_in_Greater_China" title="Pokémon in Greater China">
           Chinese
          </a>
          <a href="/wiki/Pok%C3%A9dex_entry" title="Pokédex entry">
           Pokédex entries
          </a>
          ; other-language versions use a gender-neutral word.
         </li>
        </ul>
        <h3>
         <span class="mw-headline" id="Origin">
          Origin
         </span>
        </h3>
        <p>
         Zacian may be based on
         <a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/King_Arthur" title="wp:King Arthur">
          King Arthur
         </a>
         's sword
         <a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Excalibur" title="wp:Excalibur">
          Excalibur
         </a>
         . Its role as a warrior aiding a king may take inspiration on the
         <a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Knights_of_the_Round_Table" title="wp:Knights of the Round Table">
          Knights of the Round Table
         </a>
         . In addition, its feminine nature may be a reference to the
         <a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Lady_of_the_Lake" title="wp:Lady of the Lake">
          Lady of the Lake
         </a>
         , the character responsible for giving King Arthur his sword, and its relationship with Zamazenta may allude to the relationship between King Arthur and his sister
         <a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Morgan_le_Fay" title="wp:Morgan le Fay">
          Morgan le Fay
         </a>
         . It otherwise resembles a
         <a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/wolf" title="wp:wolf">
          wolf
         </a>
         , an animal once native to
         <a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Great_Britain" title="wp:Great Britain">
          Great Britain
         </a>
         and an important heraldic symbol for noble families during the
         <a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Ages" title="wp:Middle Ages">
          Middle Ages
         </a>
         . Its long, hanging blue fur resembles a
         <a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/caparison" title="wp:caparison">
          caparison
         </a>
         , a cloth covering usually worn by warhorses during the
         <a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/High_Middle_Ages" title="wp:High Middle Ages">
          High Middle Ages
         </a>
         .
        </p>
        <p>
         The story of Zacian and Zamazenta retreating to the Slumbering Weald to recover from their wounds, and their return in the present day to save Galar, parallels the legend of
         <a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/King_Arthur%27s_messianic_return" title="wp:King Arthur's messianic return">
          King Arthur's messianic return
         </a>
         .
        </p>
        <p>
         Zacian's sword's ability to cut through anything, with Zamazenta's shield resisting any attack, could be an example of an
         <a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/irresistible_force_paradox" title="wp:irresistible force paradox">
          irresistible force paradox
         </a>
         . One of the most famous examples of this in folklore includes the Chinese tale of a peddler selling a spear and a shield with similar properties, only to be asked what would happen if the two items were to be used against one another. Another example tells of the Greek hunting hound
         <a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Laelaps_(mythology)" title="wp:Laelaps (mythology)">
          Laelaps
         </a>
         , which always caught its prey, being set upon
         <a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Teumessian_fox" title="wp:Teumessian fox">
          Teumessian fox
         </a>
         , which could never be caught, and had to be turned into constellations to prevent the paradox.
        </p>
        <p>
         Additionally, the crescent shapes on its sword while using Behemoth Blade may reference
         <a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Hati_Hr%C3%B3%C3%B0vitnisson" title="wp:Hati Hróðvitnisson">
          Hati Hróðvitnisson
         </a>
         , a wolf that chases after the Moon in Norse mythology.
        </p>
        <h4>
         <span class="mw-headline" id="Name_origin">
          Name origin
         </span>
        </h4>
        <p>
         Zacian is derived from
         <i>
          the cyan
         </i>
         .
         <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-2">
          <a href="#cite_note-2">
           [2]
          </a>
         </sup>
        </p>
        <ul>
         <li>
          The way in which "the" is transformed into "za" may be a reference to the substitution of the /ð/ phoneme ("th") to the /z/ phoneme, which is commonly made by speakers of languages which don't have the /θ/ phoneme originally, including Japanese. The substitution of "e" for "a" may also reflect the possible pronunciation of the "e" in "the" using the /ʌ/ or the /ə/ ("uh") phonemes, which may be represented by the "a" letter in many languages, including in the romanization of Japanese.
         </li>
        </ul>

        // Initialize elements
appendElementIf({id: "adthrive-left-s", wAbove: 1520, wBelow: 1699, hAbove: 700});
appendElementIf({id: "adthrive-left-m", wAbove: 1700, wBelow: 1890, hAbove: 700});

appendElementIf({id: "adthrive-right-m", wAbove: 1100, wBelow: 1399, hAbove: 964});
appendElementIf({id: "adthrive-right-l", wAbove: 1400, hAbove: 964});
appendElementIf({id: "adthrive-right-rect", hBelow: 964});


// Appends element if condition is met
function appendElementIf({id, wAbove, wBelow, hAbove, hBelow}) {

	// find browser height
	var w = window.innerWidth;
	var h = window.innerHeight;

	// If true after browser size check then unit is added
	var condition = true;

	// Check size conditions
	if (wBelow && (w > wBelow)) condition = false;
	if (wAbove && (w < wAbove)) condition = false;

	if (hBelow && (h > hBelow)) condition = false;
	if (hAbove && (h < hAbove)) condition = false;

	// Append element if condition is met
	if (condition) {
		createAndAppendElement(id);
	}
}


// creates and appends a div element to the body
function createAndAppendElement(id)
{
	var atEl = document.createElement('div');
	atEl.id = id;
	document.body.appendChild(atEl);
}
